   │ <?php\n
   │ \n
   │ // Load the necessary configuration and library files.\n
   │ require_once dirname(__FILE__) . '/../../config.php';\n
   │ require_once dirname(__FILE__) . '/lib.php';\n
   │ \n
   │ try {\n
   │ \n
   │     // Fetch and validate the necessary parameter from the request.\n
   │     $cmid = optional_param('cmid', null, PARAM_INT);\n
   │ \n
   │     // Validate course module and additional data.\n
   │     if ($cmid === null) {\n
   │         throw new moodle_exception('nocmid', 'sqlab');\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     $cm = get_coursemodule_from_id('sqlab', $cmid);\n
   │     if (!$cm) {\n
   │         throw new moodle_exception('invalidcoursemodule', 'sqlab');\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     $course = get_course($cm->course);\n
   │     if (!$course) {\n
   │         throw new moodle_exception('invalidcourseid', 'sqlab');\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     // Get and check the existence of the SQLab instance.\n
   │     $sqlab = $DB->get_record('sqlab', array('id' => $cm->instance), '*', IGNORE_MISSING);\n
   │     if (!$sqlab) {\n
   │         throw new moodle_exception('invalidsqlabid', 'sqlab');\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │ } catch (moodle_exception $e) {\n
   │ \n
   │     // Define the redirect URL.\n
   │     $redirectUrl = (!empty($course->id)) ? new moodle_url('/course/view.php', ['id' => $course->id]) : new moodle_url('/my/');\n
   │ \n
   │     \core\notification::error(get_string($e->errorcode, $e->module));\n
   │     redirect($redirectUrl);\n
   │     exit;\n
   │ \n
   │ }\n
   │ \n
   │ // Enforce course module context and user login.\n
   │ $context = context_module::instance($cm->id);\n
   │ require_login($course, true, $cm);\n
   │ \n
   │ // Check if there is a password for the activity or not.\n
   │ $passwordRequired = !empty($sqlab->activitypassword);\n
   │ \n
   │ // Check if password is required and the request method is POST.\n
   │ if ($passwordRequired && $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD'] === 'POST') {\n
   │ \n
   │     // Get password from POST data.\n
   │     $password = $_POST['password'] ?? '';\n
   │ \n
   │     // Get correct password from SQLab activity settings.\n
   │     $correctPassword = $sqlab->activitypassword;\n
   │ \n
   │     // Check if password is empty or incorrect.\n
   │     if (empty($password) || $password !== $correctPassword) {\n
   │ \n
   │         // Output JSON response for failure with error message.\n
   │         echo json_encode(['status' => 'fail', 'message' => get_string('passwordincorrect', 'sqlab')]);\n
   │ \n
   │     } else {\n
   │ \n
   │         // Output JSON response for success.\n
   │         echo json_encode(['status' => 'success']);\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │ } else {\n
   │     // Output JSON response for failure with invalid request message.\n
   │     echo json_encode(['status' => 'fail', 'message' => 'Invalid request']);\n
   │ }\n
   │ <?php\n
   │ \n
   │ // Load the necessary configuration and library files.\n
   │ require_once dirname(__FILE__) . '/../../config.php';\n
   │ require_once dirname(__FILE__) . '/lib.php';\n
   │ \n
   │ try {\n
   │ \n
   │     // Fetch necessary parameters from the request.\n
   │     $attemptId = optional_param('attempt', null, PARAM_INT);\n
   │     $questionId = optional_param('question', null, PARAM_INT);\n
   │     $cmId = optional_param('cmid', null, PARAM_INT);\n
   │     $sqlCode = optional_param('sql_code', null, PARAM_TEXT);\n
   │     $evaluate = optional_param('evaluate', null, PARAM_BOOL);\n
   │ \n
   │     // Validate that necessary parameters are provided.\n
   │     if ($attemptId === null) {\n
   │         throw new moodle_exception('noattemptid', 'sqlab');\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     if ($questionId === null) {\n
   │         throw new moodle_exception('noquestionid', 'sqlab');\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     if ($cmId === null) {\n
   │         throw new moodle_exception('nocmid', 'sqlab');\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     if ($sqlCode === null) {\n
   │         throw new moodle_exception('nosqlcode', 'sqlab');\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     if ($evaluate === null) {\n
   │         throw new moodle_exception('noevaluate', 'sqlab');\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     $cm = get_coursemodule_from_id('sqlab', $cmId);\n
   │     if (!$cm) {\n
   │         throw new moodle_exception('invalidcoursemodule', 'sqlab');\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     $course = get_course($cm->course);\n
   │     if (!$course) {\n
   │         throw new moodle_exception('invalidcourseid', 'sqlab');\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     // Get and check the existence of the SQLab instance.\n
   │     $sqlab = $DB->get_record('sqlab', array('id' => $cm->instance), '*', IGNORE_MISSING);\n
   │     if (!$sqlab) {\n
   │         throw new moodle_exception('invalidsqlabid', 'sqlab');\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     // Check the existence of attempt and obtain it.\n
   │     $attempt = $DB->get_record('sqlab_attempts', ['id' => $attemptId, 'sqlabid' => $sqlab->id, 'userid' => $USER->id], '*', IGNORE_MISSING);\n
   │     if (!$attempt) {\n
   │         throw new moodle_exception('invalidattemptid', 'sqlab');\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │ } catch (moodle_exception $e) {\n
   │ \n
   │     // Define the redirect URL based on the exception and available data.\n
   │     if ($e->errorcode === 'invalidcoursemodule' && $cmId !== null) {\n
   │         $redirectUrl = new moodle_url('/my/');\n
   │     } else if ($e->errorcode === 'invalidsqlabid') {\n
   │         $redirectUrl = new moodle_url('/my/');\n
   │     } else {\n
   │         if (!empty($cmId)) {\n
   │             $redirectUrl = new moodle_url('/mod/sqlab/view.php', ['id' => $cmId]);  // Redirect to the module's view page if cmid is available and valid.\n
   │         } else {\n
   │             $redirectUrl = (!empty($course->id)) ? new moodle_url('/course/view.php', ['id' => $course->id]) : new moodle_url('/my/');\n
   │         }\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     \core\notification::error(get_string($e->errorcode, $e->module));\n
   │     redirect($redirectUrl);\n
   │     exit;\n
   │ \n
   │ }\n
   │ \n
   │ // Enforce course module context and check capabilities.\n
   │ $context = context_module::instance($cm->id);\n
   │ require_capability('mod/sqlab:attempt', $context);\n
   │ \n
   │ // Get the related quiz questions.\n
   │ $quiz_questions = sqlab_get_quiz_questions($sqlab->quizid);\n
   │ \n
   │ // Redirection and error notification if no questions are found.\n
   │ if (empty($quiz_questions)) {\n
   │     \core\notification::error(get_string('noquestionsfound', 'sqlab'));\n
   │     redirect(new moodle_url('/mod/sqlab/view.php', ['id' => $cmId]));\n
   │     exit;\n
   │ }\n
   │ \n
   │ // Find the current question based on the ID.\n
   │ $current_question = null;\n
   │ foreach ($quiz_questions as $question) {\n
   │     if ($question['questionid'] == $questionId) {\n
   │         $current_question = $question;\n
   │         break;\n
   │     }\n
   │ }\n
   │ \n
   │ // Redirection and error notification if the question is not found.\n
   │ if (!$current_question) {\n
   │     \core\notification::error(get_string('questionnotfound', 'sqlab'));\n
   │     redirect(new moodle_url('/mod/sqlab/view.php', ['id' => $cmId]));\n
   │     exit;\n
   │ }\n
   │ \n
   │ // Check if the current request method is POST.\n
   │ if ($_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD'] === 'POST') {\n
   │ \n
   │     // Proceed if the request is for evaluation, not just code execution (the ‘Evaluate code’ button has been clicked).\n
   │     if ($evaluate) {\n
   │ \n
   │         // Check if response exists for that question in that particular attempt for that particular user.\n
   │         $response = $DB->get_record('sqlab_responses', ['attemptid' => $attemptId, 'questionid' => $questionId, 'userid' => $USER->id]);\n
   │ \n
   │         // Create a new response if it doesn't exist.\n
   │         if (!$response) {\n
   │ \n
   │             $response = new stdClass();\n
   │             $response->attemptid = $attemptId;\n
   │             $response->questionid = $questionId;\n
   │             $response->userid = $USER->id;\n
   │             $response->response = $sqlCode;\n
   │             $response->currentmaxgrade = $current_question['questiongrade'];\n
   │             $response->execution_count = 0;\n
   │             $response->timecreated = time();\n
   │             $response->timemodified = $response->timecreated;\n
   │             $DB->insert_record('sqlab_responses', $response);\n
   │ \n
   │         } else { // Update the existing response.\n
   │ \n
   │             $response->response = $sqlCode;\n
   │             $response->execution_count++;\n
   │             $response->timemodified = time();\n
   │             $DB->update_record('sqlab_responses', $response);\n
   │ \n
   │         }\n

   │         $table->data[] = $row;\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     // End the display of attempts summary.\n
   │     echo html_writer::table($table);\n
   │     echo html_writer::end_tag('div');\n

   │ \n

   │         <div class="modal-content animate-top">\n

   │ }\n

   │ <?php\n
   │ \n
   │ // Load the necessary configuration, library files and namespaces.\n
   │ require_once dirname(__FILE__) . '/../../config.php';\n
   │ require_once dirname(__FILE__) . '/lib.php';\n
   │ use mod_sqlab\user_query_executor;\n
   │ use mod_sqlab\schema_manager;\n
   │ \n
   │ // Set the content type of the response to JSON.\n
   │ header('Content-Type: application/json');\n
   │ \n
   │ try {\n
   │ \n
   │     // Ensure the request method is POST.\n
   │     if ($_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD'] !== 'POST') {\n
   │         throw new moodle_exception('invalidrequestmethod', 'sqlab');\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     // Retrieve JSON input from the request body and decode it.\n
   │     $json_input = file_get_contents('php://input');\n
   │     $input = json_decode($json_input, true);\n
   │ \n
   │     // Check if all required parameters are provided.\n
   │     if (!isset($input['attempt']) || !isset($input['sql']) || !isset($input['action'])) {\n
   │         throw new moodle_exception('missingparameters', 'sqlab');\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     // Extract parameters from the input.\n
   │     $attemptid = $input['attempt'];\n
   │     $sql = $input['sql'];\n
   │     $action = $input['action'];\n
   │ \n
   │     // Retrieve records from the database based on the provided attempt ID.\n
   │     $attempt = $DB->get_record('sqlab_attempts', ['id' => $attemptid], '*', IGNORE_MISSING);\n
   │     if (!$attempt) {\n
   │         throw new moodle_exception('invalidattemptid', 'sqlab');\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     $sqlab = $DB->get_record('sqlab', ['id' => $attempt->sqlabid], '*', IGNORE_MISSING);\n
   │     if (!$sqlab) {\n
   │         throw new moodle_exception('invalidsqlabid', 'sqlab');\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     $schemaName = schema_manager::format_activity_name($sqlab->name);\n
   │ \n
   │     // Execute the SQL query using the formatted schema name.\n
   │     $executionResults = user_query_executor::execute_user_sql($attemptid, $sql, $schemaName);\n
   │ \n
   │     // Prepare the initial response structure.\n
   │     $response = ['status' => 'success', 'results' => []];\n
   │     $resultsArray = [];\n
   │ \n
   │     // Process execution results and handle potential errors.\n
   │     foreach ($executionResults as $result) {\n
   │         if (isset($result['error'])) {\n
   │             $response['status'] = 'error';\n
   │             $response['message'] = $result['message'];\n
   │             $resultsArray[] = $result['message'];\n
   │             break;\n
   │         } else {\n
   │             $response['results'][] = $result;\n
   │             $resultsArray[] = $result;\n
   │         }\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     // Prepare a record for database insertion.\n
   │     $record = new stdClass();\n
   │     $record->userid = $USER->id;\n
   │     $record->attemptid = $attemptid;\n
   │     $record->executed_code = $sql;\n
   │     $record->action = $action;\n
   │     $record->received_reply = json_encode($resultsArray);\n
   │     $record->execution_timestamp = date('Y-m-d\TH:i:s\Z');\n
   │ \n
   │     // Insert the execution record into the database.\n
   │     $DB->insert_record('sqlab_code_executions', $record);\n
   │ \n
   │     // Output the response as JSON.\n
   │     echo json_encode($response);\n
   │ \n
   │ } catch (moodle_exception $e) {\n
   │     echo json_encode(['status' => 'error', 'message' => $e->getMessage()]);\n
   │     exit;\n
   │ }\n
   │ <?php\n
   │ \n
   │ // Prevent PHP scripts from being accessed directly from the browser.\n
   │ defined('MOODLE_INTERNAL') || die();\n
   │ \n
   │ /**\n
   │  * Determines the features supported by the SQLab module.\n
   │  *\n
   │  * @param string $feature The constant name of the feature being checked.\n
   │  * @return mixed Returns true or false for most features, specific values for certain features,\n
   │  *               or null if the feature is not recognized.\n
   │  */\n
   │ function sqlab_supports($feature)\n
   │ {\n
   │     $features = [\n
   │         FEATURE_GROUPS => false, // No support for group assignments.\n
   │         FEATURE_GROUPINGS => false, // No support for groupings.\n
   │         FEATURE_MOD_INTRO => false, // No introductory text field.\n
   │         FEATURE_COMPLETION_TRACKS_VIEWS => false, // Does not interact with completion views.\n
   │         FEATURE_COMPLETION_HAS_RULES => false, // No additional completion rules.\n
   │         FEATURE_GRADE_HAS_GRADE => true,  // Supports grades.\n
   │         FEATURE_GRADE_OUTCOMES => true,  // Supports grading outcomes.\n
   │         FEATURE_BACKUP_MOODLE2 => true,  // Supports Moodle 2 backup and restore.\n
   │         FEATURE_SHOW_DESCRIPTION => true,  // Shows description on course page.\n
   │         FEATURE_ADVANCED_GRADING => false, // No support for advanced grading methods.\n
   │         FEATURE_CONTROLS_GRADE_VISIBILITY => true  // Controls visibility of grades.\n
   │     ];\n
   │ \n
   │     if (array_key_exists($feature, $features)) {\n
   │         return $features[$feature];\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     if ($feature == FEATURE_MOD_PURPOSE && defined('FEATURE_MOD_PURPOSE')) {\n
   │         return MOD_PURPOSE_ASSESSMENT; // Defines module as 'assessment' type.\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     return null; // Feature not recognized.\n
   │ }\n
   │ \n
   │ /**\n
   │  * Adds a new SQLab instance to the database.\n
   │  *\n
   │  * @param object $data An object containing the data for the new SQLab instance, including the quiz ID.\n
   │  * @return int The ID of the newly created SQLab instance.\n
   │  * @throws coding_exception Throws exception if the Quiz ID is invalid.\n
   │  */\n
   │ function sqlab_add_instance($data)\n
   │ {\n
   │     global $DB;\n
   │ \n
   │     $data->timecreated = time();\n
   │     $data->timemodified = $data->timecreated;\n
   │ \n
   │     if (empty($data->quizid) || !is_numeric($data->quizid)) {\n
   │         throw new coding_exception('Invalid Quiz ID');\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     $id = $DB->insert_record('sqlab', $data);\n
   │ \n
   │     return $id;\n
   │ }\n
   │ \n
   │ /**\n
   │  * Updates an existing SQLab instance in the database.\n
   │  *\n
   │  * @param object $data An object containing the new data for the SQLab instance, including the instance ID.\n
   │  * @return bool Returns true upon successful update of the instance.\n
   │  * @throws coding_exception Throws exception if the instance ID is missing in the data.\n
   │  */\n
   │ function sqlab_update_instance($data)\n
   │ {\n
   │     global $DB;\n
   │ \n
   │     if (empty($data->instance)) {\n
   │         throw new coding_exception('Instance ID is missing');\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     $data->id = $data->instance;\n
   │ \n
   │     $data->timemodified = time();\n
   │ \n
   │     $DB->update_record('sqlab', $data);\n
   │ \n
   │     return true;\n
   │ }\n
   │ \n
   │ /**\n
   │  * Deletes a specific instance of an SQLab record by ID.\n
   │  *\n
   │  * @param int $id The ID of the SQLab instance to be deleted.\n
   │  * @return bool Returns true if the record was successfully deleted, false if the record does not exist.\n
   │  */\n
   │ function sqlab_delete_instance($id)\n
   │ {\n
   │     global $DB;\n
   │ \n
   │     if (!$DB->record_exists('sqlab', array('id' => $id))) {\n
   │         return false;\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     $DB->delete_records('sqlab', array('id' => $id));\n
   │ \n
   │     return true;\n
   │ }\n
   │ \n
   │ /**\n
   │  * Retrieves detailed information for all questions associated with a specific quiz.\n
   │  *\n
   │  * @param int $quizid The ID of the quiz for which questions are being retrieved.\n
   │  * @return array An array of associative arrays, each representing a quiz question's detailed information.\n
   │  */\n
   │ function sqlab_get_quiz_questions($quizid)\n
   │ {\n
   │     global $DB;\n
   │ \n
   │     $questions = [];\n
   │ \n
   │     $sql = "SELECT q.id AS questionid, q.questiontext, q.name AS questionname, q.createdby, u.firstname, u.lastname, \n
   │                 slot.maxmark AS questiongrade,\n
   │                 qso.relatedconcepts, qso.relationalschema, qso.data, qso.code, qso.resultdata, \n
   │                 qso.subjectivedifficulty, qso.objectivedifficulty, qso.solution,\n
   │                 qso.decreaseattempt, qso.mingrade, qso.sqlcheck, qso.sqlcheckrun\n
   │             FROM {quiz_slots} slot\n
   │             LEFT JOIN {question_references} qr ON qr.component = 'mod_quiz' AND qr.questionarea = 'slot' AND qr.itemid = slot.id\n
   │             LEFT JOIN {question_bank_entries} qbe ON qbe.id = qr.questionbankentryid\n
   │             LEFT JOIN (\n
   │                 SELECT qv1.questionbankentryid, qv1.questionid\n
   │                 FROM {question_versions} qv1\n
   │                 WHERE qv1.id IN (\n
   │                     SELECT MAX(qv2.id)\n
   │                     FROM {question_versions} qv2\n
   │                     GROUP BY qv2.questionbankentryid\n
   │                 )\n
   │             ) qv ON qv.questionbankentryid = qbe.id\n
   │             LEFT JOIN {question} q ON q.id = qv.questionid\n
   │             LEFT JOIN {user} u ON q.createdby = u.id\n
   │             LEFT JOIN {qtype_sqlquestion_options} qso ON qso.questionid = q.id\n
   │             WHERE slot.quizid = ?;";\n
   │ \n
   │     $params = [$quizid];\n
   │     $question_records = $DB->get_records_sql($sql, $params);\n
   │ \n
   │     foreach ($question_records as $record) {\n
   │         $questions[] = [\n
   │             'questionid' => $record->questionid,\n
   │             'statement' => $record->questiontext,\n
   │             'questionname' => $record->questionname,\n
   │             'authorid' => $record->createdby,\n
   │             'author' => $record->firstname . ' ' . $record->lastname,\n
   │             'questiongrade' => $record->questiongrade,\n
   │             'relatedconcepts' => $record->relatedconcepts,\n
   │             'relationalschema' => $record->relationalschema,\n
   │             'data' => $record->data,\n
   │             'code' => $record->code,\n
   │             'resultdata' => $record->resultdata,\n
   │             'subjectivedifficulty' => $record->subjectivedifficulty,\n
   │             'objectivedifficulty' => $record->objectivedifficulty,\n
   │             'solution' => $record->solution,\n
   │             'decreaseattempt' => $record->decreaseattempt,\n
   │             'mingrade' => $record->mingrade,\n
   │             'sqlcheck' => $record->sqlcheck,\n
   │             'sqlcheckrun' => $record->sqlcheckrun\n
   │         ];\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     return $questions;\n
   │ }\n
   │ \n
   │ /**\n
   │  * Retrieves the number of attempts for a specified quiz.\n
   │  *\n
   │  * @param int $quizid The ID of the quiz for which the attempt count is being retrieved.\n
   │  * @return int The number of attempts for the specified quiz.\n
   │  * @throws \moodle_exception Throws an exception if the quiz cannot be found in the database.\n
   │  */\n
   │ function sqlab_get_quiz_attempts_count($quizid)\n
   │ {\n
   │     global $DB;\n
   │ \n
   │     $sql = "SELECT attempts FROM {quiz} WHERE id = ?";\n
   │     $params = [$quizid];\n
   │     $quiz = $DB->get_record_sql($sql, $params);\n
   │ \n
   │     if ($quiz) {\n
   │         return $quiz->attempts;\n
   │     } else {\n
   │         throw new \moodle_exception('Quiz not found for ID: ' . $quizid);\n
   │     }\n
   │ }\n
   │ \n
   │ /**\n
   │  * Determines whether a specific question has been answered by a user within a given attempt.\n
   │  *\n
   │  * @param int $attemptid The ID of the attempt.\n
   │  * @param int $questionid The ID of the question.\n
   │  * @param int $userid The ID of the user.\n
   │  * @return bool Returns true if a valid response exists, false otherwise.\n
   │  */\n
   │ function sqlab_is_question_answered($attemptid, $questionid, $userid)\n
   │ {\n
   │     global $DB;\n
   │ \n
   │     $response = $DB->get_record(\n
   │         'sqlab_responses',\n
   │         array(\n
   │             'attemptid' => $attemptid,\n
   │             'questionid' => $questionid,\n
   │             'userid' => $userid\n
   │         )\n
   │     );\n
   │ \n
   │     return !empty($response) && !empty($response->response);\n
   │ }\n

   │             'teacher' => CAP_PREVENT,\n
   │             'editingteacher' => CAP_ALLOW,\n
   │             'coursecreator' => CAP_ALLOW,\n
   │             'manager' => CAP_ALLOW,\n
   │         ],\n
   │     ],\n
   │ \n
   │ ];\n
   │ <?php\n
   │ \n
   │ namespace mod_sqlab;\n
   │ \n
   │ defined('MOODLE_INTERNAL') || die();\n
   │ \n
   │ class encoder\n
   │ {\n
   │     private static $key = 'aN67haft53jkas4dH8L';\n
   │ \n
   │     /**\n
   │      * Encrypts data using AES-256-CBC encryption.\n
   │      *\n
   │      * @param string $data The plaintext data to encrypt.\n
   │      * @return string The encrypted data encoded in Base64.\n
   │      * @throws \InvalidArgumentException If the input data is empty.\n
   │      * @throws \RuntimeException If encryption fails.\n
   │      */\n
   │     public static function encrypt($data)\n
   │     {\n
   │         if (empty($data)) {\n
   │             throw new \InvalidArgumentException("Data to encrypt cannot be empty.");\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         // Generate a random initialization vector (IV).\n
   │         $iv = openssl_random_pseudo_bytes(openssl_cipher_iv_length('aes-256-cbc'));\n
   │ \n
   │         // Encrypt the data using OpenSSL.\n
   │         $encrypted = openssl_encrypt($data, 'aes-256-cbc', self::$key, 0, $iv);\n
   │         if ($encrypted === false) {\n
   │             throw new \RuntimeException("Encryption failed.");\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         // Return the encrypted data with IV, base64 encoded.\n
   │         return base64_encode($encrypted . '::' . $iv);\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     /**\n
   │      * Decrypts data encoded in Base64 and encrypted using AES-256-CBC.\n
   │      *\n
   │      * @param string $data The Base64-encoded encrypted data.\n
   │      * @return string The decrypted plaintext data.\n
   │      * @throws \InvalidArgumentException If the input data is empty or improperly formatted.\n
   │      * @throws \RuntimeException If decryption fails.\n
   │      */\n
   │     public static function decrypt($data)\n
   │     {\n
   │         if (empty($data) || count(explode('::', base64_decode($data), 2)) !== 2) {\n
   │             throw new \InvalidArgumentException("Invalid input data format for decryption.");\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         // Split the encrypted data and IV.\n
   │         list($encrypted_data, $iv) = explode('::', base64_decode($data), 2);\n
   │ \n
   │         // Decrypt the data using OpenSSL.\n
   │         $decrypted = openssl_decrypt($encrypted_data, 'aes-256-cbc', self::$key, 0, $iv);\n
   │         if ($decrypted === false) {\n
   │             throw new \RuntimeException("Decryption failed.");\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         return $decrypted;\n
   │     }\n
   │ }\n
   │ <?php\n
   │ \n
   │ namespace mod_sqlab;\n
   │ \n
   │ defined('MOODLE_INTERNAL') || die();\n
   │ \n
   │ class database_manager\n
   │ {\n
   │     /**\n
   │      * Retrieves the ID of a role based on its short name.\n
   │      *\n
   │      * @param string $roleShortName The short name of the role to find.\n
   │      * @return int The ID of the role.\n
   │      * @throws \moodle_exception If the role cannot be found.\n
   │      */\n
   │     public static function get_role_id_by_shortname($roleShortName)\n
   │     {\n
   │         global $DB;\n
   │ \n
   │         // Attempt to find the role in the database.\n
   │         $role = $DB->get_record('role', array('shortname' => $roleShortName), '*', IGNORE_MISSING);\n
   │ \n
   │         // If the role does not exist, throw an exception.\n
   │         if (!$role) {\n
   │             throw new \moodle_exception('rolenotfound', 'error', '', null, "Role short name: $roleShortName not found.");\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         // Return the ID of the found role.\n
   │         return $role->id;\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     /**\n
   │      * Processes a role assignment event to potentially set up a user-specific database.\n
   │      *\n
   │      * @param array $event_data Data associated with the role assignment event.\n
   │      * @throws \moodle_exception If the user cannot be found or a database error occurs.\n
   │      */\n
   │     public static function handle_role_assignment($event_data)\n
   │     {\n
   │         global $DB;\n
   │ \n
   │         try {\n
   │ \n
   │             $role_id = $event_data['objectid'];\n
   │             $user_id = $event_data['relateduserid'];\n
   │ \n
   │             // Return immediately if the assigned role is not 'student'.\n
   │             if ($role_id != self::get_role_id_by_shortname('student')) {\n
   │                 return;\n
   │             }\n
   │ \n
   │             // Retrieve user record from the database.\n
   │             $user = $DB->get_record('user', array('id' => $user_id));\n
   │             if (!$user) {\n
   │                 throw new \moodle_exception('usernotfound', 'error', '', null, "User ID: $user_id not found.");\n
   │             }\n
   │ \n
   │             // Format a database name using the user's information.\n
   │             $db_name = self::format_db_name($user->firstname, $user->lastname, $user_id);\n
   │ \n
   │             // Check if the database already exists and return if it does.\n
   │             if (self::check_database_exists($db_name)) {\n
   │                 return;\n
   │             }\n
   │ \n
   │             // Create a new database for the user if it does not exist.\n
   │             self::create_user_database($db_name, $user_id);\n
   │ \n
   │         } catch (\dml_exception $e) {\n
   │             error_log("Error in handle_role_assignment for user with ID $user_id: " . $e->getMessage());\n
   │             throw $e; // Re-throw the exception after logging it.\n
   │         }\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     /**\n
   │      * Formats a database name using a first name, last name, and user ID.\n
   │      *\n
   │      * @param string $firstname The user's first name.\n
   │      * @param string $lastname The user's last name.\n
   │      * @param int $user_id The user's ID.\n
   │      * @return string The formatted database name in uppercase.\n
   │      */\n
   │     private static function format_db_name($firstname, $lastname, $user_id)\n
   │     {\n
   │         $maxLength = 63; // Maximum length for PostgreSQL identifiers.\n
   │         $firstname = self::sanitize_name($firstname);\n
   │         $lastname = self::sanitize_name($lastname);\n
   │         $db_name = strtoupper($firstname . '_' . $lastname . '_' . $user_id);\n
   │ \n
   │         // Shorten the name parts if the combined length exceeds the maximum.\n
   │         if (strlen($db_name) > $maxLength) {\n
   │             $availableLength = $maxLength - strlen($user_id) - 2; // Account for underscores.\n
   │             $halfLength = floor($availableLength / 2);\n
   │             $shortFirstname = substr($firstname, 0, $halfLength);\n
   │             $shortLastname = substr($lastname, 0, $halfLength);\n
   │             $db_name = strtoupper($shortFirstname . '_' . $shortLastname . '_' . $user_id);\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         return $db_name;\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     /**\n
   │      * Sanitizes a name by removing non-alphanumeric characters and converting spaces to underscores.\n
   │      *\n
   │      * @param string $name The name to sanitize.\n
   │      * @return string The sanitized name.\n
   │      */\n
   │     private static function sanitize_name($name)\n
   │     {\n
   │         $name = iconv('UTF-8', 'ASCII//TRANSLIT', $name); // Convert accents and special characters to ASCII.\n
   │         $name = preg_replace('/\s+/', '_', $name); // Replace spaces with underscores.\n
   │         $name = preg_replace('/[^A-Za-z0-9_]/', '', $name); // Remove non-alphanumeric characters.\n
   │         return $name;\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     /**\n
   │      * Generates a random password of a specified length, including at least one digit, uppercase letter, lowercase letter, and special character.\n
   │      *\n
   │      * @param int $length The desired length of the password.\n
   │      * @return string The randomly generated password.\n
   │      */\n
   │     private static function generate_random_password($length = 12)\n
   │     {\n
   │         $digit = chr(mt_rand(48, 57)); // 0-9\n
   │         $upper = chr(mt_rand(65, 90)); // A-Z\n
   │         $lower = chr(mt_rand(97, 122)); // a-z\n
   │         $special_chars = '!@$%^&*-_+='; // PostgreSQL secure special characters.\n
   │         $special = $special_chars[mt_rand(0, strlen($special_chars) - 1)]; // Random special character.\n
   │ \n
   │         $seed = str_shuffle($digit . $upper . $lower . $special);\n
   │ \n
   │         for ($i = 0; $i < $length - 4; $i++) {\n
   │             $options = [$digit, $upper, $lower, $special_chars[mt_rand(0, strlen($special_chars) - 1)]];\n
   │             $seed .= $options[mt_rand(0, count($options) - 1)]; // Add additional random characters.\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         return str_shuffle($seed); // Shuffle to ensure randomness.\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     /**\n
   │      * Saves encrypted student credentials to the database.\n
   │      *\n
   │      * @param int $user_id The user ID of the student.\n
   │      * @param string $student_username The username of the student.\n
   │      * @param string $student_password The plaintext password of the student.\n
   │      * @throws \dml_exception If there is a database manipulation error.\n
   │      */\n
   │     private static function save_student_credentials($user_id, $student_username, $student_password)\n
   │     {\n
   │         global $DB;\n
   │ \n
   │         try {\n
   │ \n
   │             $encrypted_password = encoder::encrypt($student_password);\n
   │ \n
   │             $data = new \stdClass();\n
   │             $data->userid = $user_id;\n
   │             $data->username = $student_username;\n
   │             $data->password = $encrypted_password;\n
   │ \n
   │             // Insert the new credentials record into the database.\n
   │             $DB->insert_record('sqlab_db_user_credentials', $data);\n
   │ \n
   │         } catch (\dml_exception $e) {\n
   │             error_log("Error saving user credentials for user ID $user_id: " . $e->getMessage());\n
   │             throw $e; // Re-throw the exception after logging.\n
   │         }\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     /**\n
   │      * Checks if a database exists by connecting to PostgreSQL and querying the database list.\n
   │      *\n
   │      * @param string $db_name The name of the database to check.\n
   │      * @return bool Returns true if the database exists, false otherwise.\n
   │      */\n
   │     private static function check_database_exists($db_name)\n
   │     {\n
   │         $dbConnector = new dbconnector();\n
   │         $conn = $dbConnector->connect();\n
   │ \n
   │         if (!$conn) {\n
   │             error_log("Error: Unable to establish connection to check if the database $db_name exists.");\n
   │             return false;\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         $result = pg_query($conn, "SELECT 1 FROM pg_database WHERE datname = '$db_name'");\n
   │         if (!$result) {\n
   │             error_log("Error: Failed to check if the database $db_name exists: " . pg_last_error($conn));\n
   │             return false;\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         $exists = pg_num_rows($result) > 0;\n
   │         pg_free_result($result);\n
   │         $dbConnector->closeConnection();\n
   │ \n
   │         return $exists;\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     /**\n
   │      * Creates a user-specific database and associated login role with permissions.\n
   │      *\n
   │      * @param string $db_name The name of the database to be created.\n
   │      * @param int $user_id The user ID for whom the database is being created.\n
   │      */\n
   │     private static function create_user_database($db_name, $user_id)\n
   │     {\n
   │         $dbConnector = new dbconnector();\n
   │         $conn = $dbConnector->connect();\n
   │ \n
   │         if (!$conn) {\n
   │             error_log("Error: Failed to establish a connection to create the database $db_name.");\n
   │             return;\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         // Attempt to create the database.\n
   │         if (!pg_query($conn, "CREATE DATABASE \"$db_name\" WITH OWNER = postgres TEMPLATE = template0 ENCODING = 'UTF8'")) {\n
   │             error_log("Error creating the database $db_name: " . pg_last_error($conn));\n
   │             return;\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         // Generate role name and password for the database.\n
   │         $student_username = 'ROLE_' . $db_name;\n
   │         $student_password = self::generate_random_password();\n
   │ \n
   │         // Attempt to create the role.\n
   │         if (!pg_query($conn, "CREATE ROLE \"$student_username\" LOGIN PASSWORD '$student_password'")) {\n
   │             error_log("Error creating the role $student_username: " . pg_last_error($conn));\n
   │             return;\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         // Grant connection permissions to the role.\n
   │         if (!pg_query($conn, "GRANT CONNECT ON DATABASE \"$db_name\" TO \"$student_username\"")) {\n
   │             error_log("Error granting permissions to the role $student_username: " . pg_last_error($conn));\n
   │             return;\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         // Save the credentials in the database.\n
   │         self::save_student_credentials($user_id, $student_username, $student_password);\n
   │ \n
   │         // Close the database connection.\n
   │         $dbConnector->closeConnection();\n
   │     }\n
   │ }\n
   │ <?php\n
   │ \n
   │ namespace mod_sqlab;\n
   │ \n
   │ defined('MOODLE_INTERNAL') || die();\n
   │ \n
   │ class internal_sql_executor\n
   │ {\n
   │     /**\n
   │      * Execute SQL in a database, optionally fetching results, with dynamic connection control.\n
   │      *\n
   │      * @param mixed $userId User ID of the student.\n
   │      * @param string $sql SQL commands to execute.\n
   │      * @param string $schemaName Name of the schema to set for the SQL execution.\n
   │      * @param bool $fetchResults Whether to fetch and return results.\n
   │      * @param resource|null $dbConnection Optional existing database connection to use.\n
   │      * @param bool $adminFlag Whether to connect as admin (true) or as the student (false).\n
   │      * @return mixed Returns an array of results if fetching is requested, null otherwise.\n
   │      * @throws \moodle_exception Throws exceptions for connection or execution errors.\n
   │      */\n
   │     public static function execute($userId, $sql, $schemaName, $fetchResults = false, $dbConnection = null, $adminFlag = true)\n
   │     {\n
   │         global $DB;\n
   │         $ownConnection = false; // To track if we've created the connection ourselves.\n
   │ \n
   │         if (empty($sql)) {\n
   │             return; // No SQL to execute.\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         // Use existing connection if provided, otherwise create a new one.\n
   │         if (!$dbConnection) {\n
   │ \n
   │             // Fetch user credentials from the database.\n
   │             $credentials = $DB->get_record('sqlab_db_user_credentials', ['userid' => $userId]);\n
   │             if (!$credentials) {\n
   │                 throw new \moodle_exception('credentialsnotfound', 'mod_sqlab', '', null, "Credentials not found for user ID $userId");\n
   │             }\n
   │ \n
   │             // Determine the database name from the student's credentials.\n
   │             $studentDbName = str_replace("ROLE_", "", $credentials->username);\n
   │ \n
   │             // Connect to the database as admin or student depending on adminFlag.\n
   │             if ($adminFlag) {\n
   │                 // Admin uses default configured credentials in dbconnector.\n
   │                 $dbConnector = new dbconnector($studentDbName);\n
   │             } else {\n
   │                 // Student uses specific credentials.\n
   │                 $dbConnector = new dbconnector($studentDbName, $credentials->username, encoder::decrypt($credentials->password));\n
   │             }\n
   │ \n
   │             // Attempt to connect to the database.\n
   │             $dbConnection = $dbConnector->connect();\n
   │             $ownConnection = true; // Mark that we own this connection.\n
   │ \n
   │             if (!$dbConnection) {\n
   │                 throw new \moodle_exception('dbconnectionerror', 'mod_sqlab', '', null, "Error connecting to the database for user ID $userId");\n
   │             }\n
   │ \n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         try {\n
   │ \n
   │             // Execute SQL with transaction control for integrity.\n
   │             pg_query($dbConnection, "BEGIN");\n
   │ \n
   │             // Set the search path to the specified schema.\n
   │             pg_query($dbConnection, "SET search_path TO \"$schemaName\"");\n
   │ \n
   │             // Execute the SQL command and optionally fetch results.\n
   │             $result = self::execute_sql($dbConnection, $sql, $fetchResults);\n
   │ \n
   │             // Commit the transaction.\n
   │             pg_query($dbConnection, "COMMIT");\n
   │ \n
   │             return $result; // Return results if fetchResults is true, otherwise null.\n
   │ \n
   │         } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
   │             // Rollback the transaction in case of an error.\n
   │             pg_query($dbConnection, "ROLLBACK");\n
   │             throw new \moodle_exception('dbexecutionerror', 'mod_sqlab', '', null, $e->getMessage());\n
   │         } finally {\n
   │             if ($ownConnection && $dbConnection) {\n
   │                 // Only close the connection if we created it.\n
   │                 $dbConnector->closeConnection();\n
   │             }\n
   │         }\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     /**\n
   │      * Executes SQL queries on the given database connection and handles result fetching.\n
   │      *\n
   │      * @param resource $dbConnection Database connection resource.\n
   │      * @param string $sql SQL command to execute.\n
   │      * @param bool $fetchResults Flag indicating whether results should be fetched.\n
   │      * @return mixed Returns fetched results if requested, otherwise null.\n
   │      * @throws \Exception Throws exception on query failure.\n
   │      */\n
   │     private static function execute_sql($dbConnection, $sql, $fetchResults = false)\n
   │     {\n
   │         $result = pg_query($dbConnection, $sql);\n
   │ \n
   │         if (!$result) {\n
   │             throw new \Exception("Failed to execute SQL: " . pg_last_error($dbConnection));\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         return $fetchResults ? pg_fetch_all($result) : null;\n
   │     }\n
   │ }\n
   │ <?php\n
   │ \n
   │ namespace mod_sqlab;\n
   │ \n
   │ defined('MOODLE_INTERNAL') || die();\n
   │ \n
   │ class schema_manager\n
   │ {\n
   │     /**\n
   │      * Handles the first attempt for a user in a specific SQLab activity.\n
   │      *\n
   │      * @param int $attemptid The ID of the user's attempt.\n
   │      * @param int $userid The ID of the user.\n
   │      * @throws \moodle_exception Throws exceptions if the attempt, activity, user credentials, or database connection cannot be found or established.                          \n
   │      */\n
   │     public static function handle_first_attempt($attemptid, $userid)\n
   │     {\n
   │         global $DB;\n
   │ \n
   │         // Verify and retrieve the attempt record.\n
   │         $attempt = $DB->get_record('sqlab_attempts', ['id' => $attemptid]);\n
   │ \n
   │         if (!$attempt) {\n
   │             throw new \moodle_exception('attemptnotfound', 'sqlab', '', null, "Attempt $attemptid not found");\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         // Verify and retrieve the associated SQLab activity.\n
   │         $sqlab = $DB->get_record('sqlab', ['id' => $attempt->sqlabid]);\n
   │ \n
   │         if (!$sqlab) {\n
   │             throw new \moodle_exception('activitynotfound', 'sqlab', '', null, "Activity associated with attempt $attemptid not found");\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         $activityName = self::format_activity_name($sqlab->name);\n
   │ \n
   │         // Verify and retrieve user credentials.\n
   │         $credentials = $DB->get_record('sqlab_db_user_credentials', ['userid' => $userid]);\n
   │ \n
   │         if (!$credentials) {\n
   │             throw new \moodle_exception('credentialsnotfound', 'sqlab', '', null, "Credentials not found for user $userid");\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         // The student's database name is the username (without the "ROLE_" prefix) from the credentials.\n
   │         $studentDbName = str_replace("ROLE_", "", $credentials->username);\n
   │ \n
   │         // Connect to the student's database using administrator credentials.\n
   │         $dbConnector = new dbconnector($studentDbName);\n
   │         $studentDBConnection = $dbConnector->connect();\n
   │ \n
   │         if (!$studentDBConnection) {\n
   │             throw new \moodle_exception('dbconnectionerror', 'sqlab', '', null, "Error connecting to the student database $studentDbName");\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         // Create schema and assign permissions.\n
   │         self::create_schema_for_activity($studentDBConnection, $activityName, $credentials->username);\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     /**\n
   │      * Creates a schema for a specific activity and assigns necessary permissions to a user.\n
   │      *\n
   │      * @param resource $dbConnection The database connection resource.\n
   │      * @param string $activityName The name of the schema.\n
   │      * @param string $username The username to whom the permissions will be granted.\n
   │      * @throws \moodle_exception Throws an exception if there is an error during schema creation or permission assignment.\n
   │      */\n
   │     public static function create_schema_for_activity($dbConnection, $activityName, $username)\n
   │     {\n
   │         try {\n
   │             pg_query($dbConnection, "CREATE SCHEMA \"$activityName\"");\n
   │             pg_query($dbConnection, "GRANT USAGE ON SCHEMA \"$activityName\" TO \"$username\"");\n
   │             pg_query($dbConnection, "GRANT CREATE ON SCHEMA \"$activityName\" TO \"$username\"");\n
   │             pg_query($dbConnection, "ALTER DEFAULT PRIVILEGES IN SCHEMA \"$activityName\" GRANT ALL ON TABLES TO \"$username\"");\n
   │         } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
   │             throw new \moodle_exception('schemacreationerror', 'sqlab', '', null, "Error creating or assigning permissions in schema: " . $e->getMessage());\n
   │         }\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     /**\n
   │      * Formats an activity name to a standard database schema name format.\n
   │      *\n
   │      * @param string $name The original name of the activity.\n
   │      * @return string The formatted schema name.\n
   │      */\n
   │     public static function format_activity_name($name)\n
   │     {\n
   │         $name = iconv('UTF-8', 'ASCII//TRANSLIT', $name); // Transliterate to ASCII.\n
   │         $name = preg_replace('/\s+/', '_', $name); // Replace spaces with underscores.\n
   │         $name = preg_replace('/[^A-Za-z0-9_]/', '', $name); // Remove non-alphanumeric characters.\n
   │         return strtoupper($name); // Convert to uppercase.\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     /**\n
   │      * Drops a schema from the database if it exists.\n
   │      *\n
   │      * @param resource $dbConnection The database connection resource.\n
   │      * @param string $schemaName The name of the schema to be dropped.\n
   │      * @throws \moodle_exception Throws an exception if there is an error during the schema deletion.\n
   │      */\n
   │     public static function drop_schema($dbConnection, $schemaName)\n
   │     {\n
   │         try {\n
   │             // Attempt to drop the schema if it exists, including all contained objects.\n
   │             pg_query($dbConnection, "DROP SCHEMA IF EXISTS \"$schemaName\" CASCADE");\n
   │         } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
   │             throw new \moodle_exception('schemadeletionerror', 'sqlab', '', null, "Error dropping schema: " . $e->getMessage());\n
   │         }\n
   │     }\n
   │ }\n
   │ <?php\n
   │ \n
   │ namespace mod_sqlab;\n
   │ \n
   │ defined('MOODLE_INTERNAL') || die();\n
   │ \n
   │ class observer\n

   │      */\n
   │     public static function handle_role_assigned($event)\n
   │     {\n

   │     }\n

   │ namespace mod_sqlab\privacy;\n

   │ use core_privacy\local\metadata\collection;\n
   │ use core_privacy\local\request\user_preference_provider;\n

   │ \n
   │ /**\n
   │  * Privacy provider for the SQLab plugin, implementing null_provider and user_preference_provider.\n
   │  * \n
   │  * The SQLab plugin does not store any personal data directly. \n
   │  * However, it interfaces with user preferences and provides utilities to manage these settings.\n
   │  */\n
   │ class provider implements null_provider, user_preference_provider {\n
   │ \n
   │     /**\n
   │      * Returns a string explanation that this plugin does not store any personal data.\n
   │      *\n
   │      * @return string A language string identifier.\n
   │      */\n
   │     public static function get_reason(): string {\n
   │         return 'privacy:metadata';\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     /**\n
   │      * Returns metadata about the personal data stored by the SQLab plugin.\n
   │      *\n

   │      * @return collection The updated collection of metadata items.\n
   │      */\n
   │     public static function get_metadata(collection $items): collection {\n
   │         // SQLab stores user preferences related to user interface settings.\n
   │         $items->add_user_preference('mod_sqlab_user_setting', 'privacy:metadata:preference:description');\n
   │ \n
   │         return $items;\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     /**\n
   │      * Exports user preferences controlled by the SQLab plugin.\n
   │      *\n
