   │      */\n
   │     public static function export_user_preferences(int $userid) {\n
   │         // Fetch user's specific preferences for SQLab.\n
   │         $preference_name = 'mod_sqlab_user_setting';\n
   │         $preference_value = get_user_preferences($preference_name, null, $userid);\n
   │ \n
   │         if ($preference_value !== null) {\n
   │             writer::export_user_preference(\n
   │                 'mod_sqlab',\n
   │                 $preference_name,\n
   │                 $preference_value,\n
   │                 get_string('privacy:metadata:preference:description', 'sqlab')\n
   │             );\n
   │         }\n
   │     }\n
   │ }\n
   │ <?php\n
   │ \n
   │ namespace mod_sqlab;\n
   │ \n
   │ defined('MOODLE_INTERNAL') || die();\n
   │ \n
   │ class dbconnector\n
   │ {\n
   │     private $host;\n
   │     private $port;\n
   │     private $dbname;\n
   │     private $user;\n
   │     private $password;\n
   │     private $conn = null; // Holds the active database connection.\n
   │ \n
   │     /**\n
   │      * Constructs a new dbconnector instance with optional connection parameters.\n
   │      *\n
   │      * @param string $dbname The name of the database to connect to.\n
   │      * @param string $user The username for the database connection.\n
   │      * @param string $password The password for the database connection.\n
   │      * @param string $host The host of the database server.\n
   │      * @param string $port The port of the database server.\n
   │      */\n
   │     public function __construct($dbname = 'postgres', $user = 'postgres', $password = 'postgres', $host = 'postgres', $port = '5432')\n
   │     {\n
   │         $this->host = $host;\n
   │         $this->port = $port;\n
   │         $this->dbname = $dbname;\n
   │         $this->user = $user;\n
   │         $this->password = $password;\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     /**\n
   │      * Establishes a connection to the database using the provided credentials.\n
   │      *\n
   │      * @return resource|null The database connection resource if successful, or null if the connection fails.\n
   │      */\n
   │     public function connect()\n
   │     {\n
   │         if ($this->conn === null) {\n
   │ \n
   │             // Prepare connection string and attempt to establish a PostgreSQL connection.\n
   │             $connectionString = "host={$this->host} port={$this->port} dbname={$this->dbname} user={$this->user} password={$this->password}";\n
   │             $this->conn = pg_connect($connectionString);\n
   │ \n
   │             if (!$this->conn) {\n
   │                 error_log("Database connection error: " . pg_last_error());\n
   │                 return null;\n
   │             }\n
   │ \n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         return $this->conn;\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     /**\n
   │      * Closes the active database connection if one exists.\n
   │      */\n
   │     public function closeConnection()\n
   │     {\n
   │         if ($this->conn !== null) {\n
   │             pg_close($this->conn);\n
   │             $this->conn = null; // Reset the connection to ensure it's no longer usable.\n
   │         }\n
   │     }\n
   │ }\n
   │ <?php\n
   │ \n
   │ namespace mod_sqlab;\n
   │ \n
   │ defined('MOODLE_INTERNAL') || die();\n
   │ \n
   │ class user_query_executor\n
   │ {\n
   │     // List of SQL keywords to ignore while processing queries.\n
   │     protected static $ignoreConnectors = [\n
   │         'OR',\n
   │         'REPLACE',\n
   │         'AND',\n
   │         'ON',\n
   │         'LIMIT',\n
   │         'WHERE',\n
   │         'JOIN',\n
   │         'GROUP',\n
   │         'ORDER',\n
   │         'OPTION',\n
   │         'LEFT',\n
   │         'INNER',\n
   │         'RIGHT',\n
   │         'OUTER',\n
   │         'SET',\n
   │         'HAVING',\n
   │         'VALUES'\n
   │     ];\n
   │ \n
   │     /**\n
   │      * Detects the types of SQL statements within a provided SQL query.\n
   │      *\n
   │      * @param string $sql The complete SQL query string from which types of statements are to be detected.\n
   │      * @return array An array listing the detected types of the SQL statements.\n
   │      */\n
   │     private static function detectQueryType($sql)\n
   │     {\n
   │         // Remove SQL comments to prepare the string for processing.\n
   │         $sql = preg_replace('/(--.*)|(\s*\/\*[\s\S]*?\*\/)/', '', $sql);\n
   │ \n
   │         // Split the cleaned SQL into individual statements for further analysis.\n
   │         $statements = self::splitSqlStatements($sql);\n
   │         $queryTypes = [];\n
   │ \n
   │         // Iterate through each statement to determine its type.\n
   │         foreach ($statements as $statement) {\n
   │             if (trim($statement)) {\n
   │                 // Detect and record the type of the SQL statement.\n
   │                 $queryType = self::detectStatementType($statement);\n
   │                 $queryTypes[] = $queryType;\n
   │             }\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         // Return the list of detected SQL statement types.\n
   │         return $queryTypes;\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     /**\n
   │      * Splits the provided SQL into individual statements.\n
   │      * Handles special SQL blocks (functions, triggers) and regular SQL statements.\n
   │      *\n
   │      * @param string $sql The SQL string cleaned of comments and unnecessary connectors.\n
   │      * @return array An array containing individual SQL statements, properly ordered.\n
   │      */\n
   │     private static function splitSqlStatements($sql)\n
   │     {\n
   │         $statements = [];\n
   │ \n
   │         // Remove common SQL connectors to simplify the remaining string for further processing.\n
   │         $sql = preg_replace('/\b(' . implode('|', self::$ignoreConnectors) . ')\b/i', '', $sql);\n
   │ \n
   │         // Patterns to identify complex SQL constructs like stored functions and triggers.\n
   │         $patterns = [\n
   │             '/CREATE\s+FUNCTION\s+[\s\S]+?\$\$[\s\S]*?\$\$\s*LANGUAGE\s*plpgsql\s*;/i', // Matches PostgreSQL-style stored functions.\n
   │             '/CREATE\s+TRIGGER\s+[\s\S]+?EXECUTE\s+PROCEDURE\s+[\s\S]+?;/i' // Matches SQL triggers up to the EXECUTE PROCEDURE part.\n
   │         ];\n
   │ \n
   │         // Extract special SQL blocks based on predefined patterns and store their positions for sequential processing.\n
   │         $blocks = [];\n
   │         foreach ($patterns as $pattern) {\n
   │             preg_match_all($pattern, $sql, $matches, PREG_OFFSET_CAPTURE);\n
   │             foreach ($matches[0] as $match) {\n
   │                 $blocks[] = ['sql' => $match[0], 'start' => $match[1], 'end' => $match[1] + strlen($match[0])];\n
   │             }\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         // Sort identified blocks to maintain the natural order of SQL statements in the script.\n
   │         usort($blocks, function ($a, $b) {\n
   │             return $a['start'] - $b['start'];\n
   │         });\n
   │ \n
   │         // Reconstruct the full list of SQL statements, ensuring all code blocks are integrated in their original order.\n
   │         $lastPos = 0;\n
   │         foreach ($blocks as $block) {\n
   │             // Add SQL code found before each block.\n
   │             $intermediateSql = substr($sql, $lastPos, $block['start'] - $lastPos);\n
   │             $statements = array_merge($statements, self::extractStatements($intermediateSql));\n
   │             // Add the block itself.\n
   │             $statements[] = $block['sql'];\n
   │             $lastPos = $block['end'];\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         // Append any SQL code that follows the last block.\n
   │         $remainingSql = substr($sql, $lastPos);\n
   │         $statements = array_merge($statements, self::extractStatements($remainingSql));\n
   │ \n
   │         return $statements;\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     /**\n
   │      * Splits a given SQL string into individual statements based on the semicolon delimiter.\n
   │      *\n
   │      * @param string $sql The segment of SQL code to be split into distinct statements.\n
   │      * @return array An array of cleanly trimmed SQL statements, each terminated with a semicolon.\n
   │      */\n
   │     private static function extractStatements($sql)\n
   │     {\n
   │         $result = [];\n
   │ \n
   │         // Use a regex to split the SQL string at semicolons, only if they are not within quotes or comments.\n
   │         foreach (preg_split('/;(?=(?:[^\'"]|\'[^\']*\'|"[^"]*")*$)/', $sql) as $stmt) {\n
   │             $trimmed = trim($stmt);\n
   │             if ($trimmed) {\n
   │                 // Ensure each statement ends with a semicolon for correct SQL syntax.\n
   │                 $result[] = $trimmed . ';';\n
   │             }\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         return $result;\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     /**\n
   │      * Determines the SQL command type of a given SQL statement by examining its starting keyword.\n
   │      *\n
   │      * @param string $statement The single SQL statement to analyze.\n
   │      * @return string The type of the SQL command (e.g., 'CREATE TABLE', 'DROP INDEX') or 'UNKNOWN' if no match is found.\n
   │      */\n
   │     private static function detectStatementType($statement)\n
   │     {\n
   │         $normalizedStatement = strtoupper(trim($statement));\n
   │ \n
   │         // Define patterns for SQL command types for CREATE, DROP, and ALTER operations.\n
   │         $commandPatterns = [\n
   │             'CREATE' => [\n
   │                 'FUNCTION' => '/^CREATE\s+FUNCTION/i',\n
   │                 'TRIGGER' => '/^CREATE\s+TRIGGER/i',\n
   │                 'TABLE' => '/^CREATE\s+TABLE/i',\n
   │                 'INDEX' => '/^CREATE\s+INDEX/i',\n
   │                 'SEQUENCE' => '/^CREATE\s+SEQUENCE/i',\n
   │                 'VIEW' => '/^CREATE\s+VIEW/i',\n
   │                 'DOMAIN' => '/^CREATE\s+DOMAIN/i'\n
   │             ],\n
   │             'DROP' => [\n
   │                 'FUNCTION' => '/^DROP\s+FUNCTION/i',\n
   │                 'TRIGGER' => '/^DROP\s+TRIGGER/i',\n
   │                 'TABLE' => '/^DROP\s+TABLE/i',\n
   │                 'INDEX' => '/^DROP\s+INDEX/i',\n
   │                 'SEQUENCE' => '/^DROP\s+SEQUENCE/i',\n
   │                 'VIEW' => '/^DROP\s+VIEW/i',\n
   │                 'DOMAIN' => '/^DROP\s+DOMAIN/i'\n
   │             ],\n
   │             'ALTER' => [\n
   │                 'FUNCTION' => '/^ALTER\s+FUNCTION/i',\n
   │                 'TRIGGER' => '/^ALTER\s+TRIGGER/i',\n
   │                 'TABLE' => '/^ALTER\s+TABLE/i',\n
   │                 'INDEX' => '/^ALTER\s+INDEX/i',\n
   │                 'SEQUENCE' => '/^ALTER\s+SEQUENCE/i',\n
   │                 'VIEW' => '/^ALTER\s+VIEW/i',\n
   │                 'DOMAIN' => '/^ALTER\s+DOMAIN/i'\n
   │             ]\n
   │         ];\n
   │ \n
   │         // Iterate through the command patterns to find a match for the normalized statement.\n
   │         foreach ($commandPatterns as $command => $patterns) {\n
   │             foreach ($patterns as $type => $pattern) {\n
   │                 if (preg_match($pattern, $normalizedStatement)) {\n
   │                     return $command . ' ' . $type; // Return the match as a concatenated string of command and type.\n
   │                 }\n
   │             }\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         // List of additional common SQL commands to check.\n
   │         $otherCommands = [\n
   │             'SELECT',\n
   │             'INSERT',\n
   │             'UPDATE',\n
   │             'DELETE',\n
   │             'GRANT',\n
   │             'REVOKE',\n
   │             'ROLLBACK',\n
   │             'SAVEPOINT',\n
   │             'SET',\n
   │             'COPY',\n
   │             'ANALYZE',\n
   │             'EXPLAIN',\n
   │             'VACUUM',\n
   │             'TRUNCATE',\n
   │             'LISTEN',\n
   │             'NOTIFY',\n
   │             'MOVE',\n
   │             'FETCH',\n
   │             'PREPARE',\n
   │             'EXECUTE',\n
   │             'DECLARE',\n
   │             'BEGIN',\n
   │             'COMMIT',\n
   │             'DROP',\n
   │             'ALTER',\n
   │             'LOCK',\n
   │             'RELEASE'\n
   │         ];\n
   │ \n
   │         // Check for other common SQL keywords.\n
   │         foreach ($otherCommands as $keyword) {\n
   │             if (strpos($normalizedStatement, $keyword) === 0) {\n
   │                 return $keyword; // Return the keyword if it matches the beginning of the statement.\n
   │             }\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         // Return 'UNKNOWN' if no known SQL command patterns are matched.\n
   │         return 'UNKNOWN';\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     /**\n
   │      * Executes SQL statements for a specified attempt and schema, handling database connection and execution.\n
   │      *\n
   │      * @param int $attemptid The unique identifier of the attempt for which SQL is executed.\n
   │      * @param string $sql The SQL statement or multiple statements to be executed.\n
   │      * @param string $schemaName The schema name to set for the execution context.\n
   │      * @return array An array containing results or error information for each executed statement.\n
   │      * @throws moodle_exception Throws exceptions for various failures such as empty SQL, missing credentials, or database connection errors.\n
   │      */\n
   │     public static function execute_user_sql($attemptid, $sql, $schemaName)\n
   │     {\n
   │         global $DB;\n
   │ \n
   │         // Ensure SQL is not empty.\n
   │         if (empty($sql)) {\n
   │             throw new moodle_exception('emptyquery', 'mod_sqlab');\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         // Retrieve attempt and user credentials records.\n
   │         $attempt = $DB->get_record('sqlab_attempts', ['id' => $attemptid], '*', MUST_EXIST);\n
   │         $credentials = $DB->get_record('sqlab_db_user_credentials', ['userid' => $attempt->userid], '*', MUST_EXIST);\n
   │ \n
   │         // Handle missing credentials.\n
   │         if (!$credentials) {\n
   │             throw new moodle_exception('credentialsnotfound', 'mod_sqlab');\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         // Decrypt password and establish database connection.\n
   │         $decrypted_password = encoder::decrypt($credentials->password);\n
   │         $studentDbName = str_replace("ROLE_", "", $credentials->username);\n
   │         $dbConnector = new dbconnector($studentDbName, $credentials->username, $decrypted_password);\n
   │         $conn = $dbConnector->connect();\n
   │ \n
   │         // Handle connection failure.\n
   │         if (!$conn) {\n
   │             throw new moodle_exception('dbconnectionerror', 'mod_sqlab');\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         try {\n
   │ \n
   │             // Set the search path to the specified schema.\n
   │             pg_query($conn, "SET search_path TO \"$schemaName\"");\n
   │             pg_send_query($conn, $sql);\n
   │ \n
   │             $combinedResults = [];\n
   │             $queryTypes = self::detectQueryType($sql);\n
   │             $queryIndex = 0;\n
   │ \n
   │             // Fetch results for each query executed.\n
   │             while ($result = pg_get_result($conn)) {\n
   │                 $queryType = $queryTypes[$queryIndex++] ?? 'UNKNOWN';\n
   │                 $state = pg_result_error_field($result, PGSQL_DIAG_SQLSTATE);\n
   │ \n
   │                 if ($state) {\n
   │                     $errorMsg = pg_result_error($result);\n
   │                     $combinedResults[] = [\n
   │                         'error' => true,\n
   │                         'message' => $errorMsg,\n
   │                         'sqlstate' => $state\n
   │                     ];\n
   │                 } else {\n
   │                     $individualResultData = pg_fetch_all($result) ?: [];\n
   │                     $affectedRows = pg_affected_rows($result);\n
   │                     $combinedResults[] = [\n
   │                         'data' => $individualResultData,\n
   │                         'affectedRows' => $affectedRows,\n
   │                         'type' => $queryType\n
   │                     ];\n
   │                 }\n
   │             }\n
   │ \n
   │             return $combinedResults;\n
   │ \n
   │         } finally {\n
   │             // Ensure the database connection is closed.\n
   │             $dbConnector->closeConnection();\n
   │         }\n
   │     }\n
   │ }\n
   │ <?php\n
   │ \n
   │ namespace mod_sqlab;\n
   │ \n
   │ defined('MOODLE_INTERNAL') || die();\n
   │ \n
   │ class attempt_manager\n
   │ {\n
   │     const IN_PROGRESS = 'inprogress';\n
   │     const FINISHED = 'finished';\n
   │     const OVERDUE = 'overdue';\n
   │ \n
   │     /**\n
   │      * Creates a new attempt for the user specified in the given SQLab activity.\n
   │      *\n
   │      * @param int $sqlabid The ID of the SQLab activity.\n
   │      * @param int $userid The ID of the user attempting the activity.\n
   │      * @return int The ID of the newly created attempt.\n
   │      * @throws \dml_exception If a database error occurs.\n
   │      */\n
   │     public static function create_new_attempt($sqlabid, $userid)\n
   │     {\n
   │         global $DB;\n
   │ \n
   │         try {\n
   │ \n
   │             // Check if an attempt already exists for the user.\n
   │             $attempts = $DB->get_records('sqlab_attempts', array('sqlabid' => $sqlabid, 'userid' => $userid), 'attempt DESC');\n
   │             $lastattempt = reset($attempts);\n
   │ \n
   │             // Determine the number of the next attempt.\n
   │             $attemptnumber = $lastattempt ? $lastattempt->attempt + 1 : 1;\n
   │ \n
   │             $record = new \stdClass();\n
   │             $record->sqlabid = $sqlabid;\n
   │             $record->userid = $userid;\n
   │             $record->attempt = $attemptnumber;\n
   │             $record->state = self::IN_PROGRESS;\n
   │             $record->timestart = time();\n
   │             $record->timefinish = 0; // 0 means that the attempt has not yet been completed.\n
   │             $record->timemodified = time();\n
   │             $record->sumgrades = 0; // Initially, there is no qualification.\n
   │ \n
   │             // Insert new attempt into the database.\n
   │             $newattemptid = $DB->insert_record('sqlab_attempts', $record);\n
   │ \n
   │             return $newattemptid;\n
   │ \n
   │         } catch (\dml_exception $e) {\n
   │             error_log("Error creating new attempt for user ID $userid at SQLab ID $sqlabid: " . $e->getMessage());\n
   │             throw $e;\n
   │         }\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     /**\n
   │      * Finalizes an in-progress attempt, marking it as finished and recording the finish time.\n
   │      *\n
   │      * @param int $attemptid The ID of the attempt to finalize.\n
   │      * @return bool True if the attempt was successfully finalized, false if no update was necessary.\n
   │      * @throws \dml_exception If a database error occurs.\n
   │      */\n
   │     public static function finalize_attempt($attemptid)\n
   │     {\n
   │         global $DB;\n
   │ \n
   │         try {\n
   │ \n
   │             // Fetch the current attempt record.\n
   │             $attempt = $DB->get_record('sqlab_attempts', array('id' => $attemptid), '*');\n
   │ \n
   │             if (!$attempt) {\n
   │                 throw new \moodle_exception('Attempt not found for ID: ' . $attemptid);\n
   │             }\n
   │ \n
   │             // Only finalize if the attempt is still in progress.\n
   │             if ($attempt->state == self::IN_PROGRESS) {\n
   │                 $attempt->state = self::FINISHED;\n
   │                 $attempt->timefinish = time(); // Set the finish time to the current time.\n
   │                 $attempt->timemodified = time(); // Update the modified time.\n
   │ \n
   │                 // Update the attempt record in the database.\n
   │                 $DB->update_record('sqlab_attempts', $attempt);\n
   │             } else {\n
   │                 error_log("Attempt with ID $attemptid is not in progress and cannot be finalized.");\n
   │                 return false;\n
   │             }\n
   │ \n
   │             return true; // Return true indicating successful finalization.\n
   │ \n
   │         } catch (\dml_exception $e) {\n
   │             error_log("Error finalizing attempt with ID $attemptid: " . $e->getMessage());\n
   │             throw $e;\n
   │         }\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     /**\n
   │      * Updates the state of a specific attempt.\n
   │      *\n
   │      * @param int $attemptid The ID of the attempt to update.\n
   │      * @param string $newstate The new state to set for the attempt.\n
   │      * @throws \dml_exception If a database error occurs.\n
   │      */\n
   │     public static function update_attempt_state($attemptid, $newstate)\n
   │     {\n
   │         global $DB;\n
   │ \n
   │         try {\n
   │ \n
   │             $record = new \stdClass();\n
   │             $record->id = $attemptid;\n
   │             $record->state = $newstate;\n
   │             $record->timemodified = time();\n
   │ \n
   │             $DB->update_record('sqlab_attempts', $record);\n
   │ \n
   │         } catch (\dml_exception $e) {\n
   │             error_log("Error updating attempt state for ID $attemptid to $newstate: " . $e->getMessage());\n
   │             throw $e;\n
   │         }\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     /**\n
   │      * Retrieves the current state of an attempt.\n
   │      *\n
   │      * @param int $attemptid The ID of the attempt whose state is to be checked.\n
   │      * @return string The current state of the attempt.\n
   │      * @throws \moodle_exception If the attempt is not found.\n
   │      */\n
   │     public static function check_attempt_state($attemptid)\n
   │     {\n
   │         global $DB;\n
   │ \n
   │         $attempt = $DB->get_record('sqlab_attempts', array('id' => $attemptid), 'state');\n
   │ \n
   │         if (!$attempt) {\n
   │             throw new \moodle_exception('Attempt not found: ' . $attemptid);\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         return $attempt->state;\n
   │     }\n
   │ }\n
   │ <?php\n
   │ \n
   │ namespace mod_sqlab;\n
   │ \n
   │ defined('MOODLE_INTERNAL') || die();\n
   │ \n
   │ class grader\n
   │ {\n
   │     /**\n
   │      * Grades a specific attempt based on its ID by evaluating the answers to its associated questions.\n
   │      *\n
   │      * @param int $attemptid The ID of the attempt to grade.\n
   │      * @throws \moodle_exception Throws moodle_exception for specific errors controlled by the application.\n
   │      * @throws \Exception Throws generic Exception for uncontrolled or external errors.\n
   │      */\n
   │     public static function gradeAttempt($attemptid)\n
   │     {\n
   │         global $DB;\n
   │ \n
   │         // Load the attempt details.\n
   │         $attempt = $DB->get_record('sqlab_attempts', ['id' => $attemptid]);\n
   │         if (!$attempt) {\n
   │             throw new \moodle_exception('attemptnotfound', 'sqlab');\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         // Retrieve the responses for the attempt.\n
   │         $questions = $DB->get_records('sqlab_responses', ['attemptid' => $attemptid, 'userid' => $attempt->userid]);\n
   │ \n
   │         // Load the SQLab instance data.\n
   │         $sqlab = $DB->get_record('sqlab', ['id' => $attempt->sqlabid]);\n
   │         if (!$sqlab) {\n
   │             throw new \moodle_exception('sqlabnotfound', 'sqlab');\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         // Validate the schema name.\n
   │         $schemaName = schema_manager::format_activity_name($sqlab->name);\n
   │         if (empty($schemaName)) {\n
   │             throw new \moodle_exception('schemanameerror', 'sqlab');\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         // Prepare database connection using user's specific credentials.\n
   │         $userCredentials = $DB->get_record('sqlab_db_user_credentials', ['userid' => $attempt->userid]);\n
   │         if (!$userCredentials) {\n
   │             throw new \moodle_exception('nocredentials', 'sqlab');\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         $studentDbName = str_replace("ROLE_", "", $userCredentials->username);\n
   │         $dbConnector = new dbconnector($studentDbName);\n
   │         $studentDBConnection = $dbConnector->connect();\n
   │ \n
   │         if (!$studentDBConnection) {\n
   │             throw new \moodle_exception('dbconnectionerror', 'sqlab');\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         try {\n
   │ \n
   │             // Initialize flag to prevent schema deletion on error.\n
   │             $deleteSchema = false;\n
   │ \n
   │             // Remove the existing scheme to ensure a clean state of the scheme.\n
   │             schema_manager::drop_schema($studentDBConnection, $schemaName);\n
   │ \n
   │             // Recreate the scheme, preparing it to evaluate the attempt.\n
   │             schema_manager::create_schema_for_activity($studentDBConnection, $schemaName, $userCredentials->username);\n
   │ \n
   │             // Initialize total grade for the attempt.\n
   │             $totalGrade = 0.0;\n
   │ \n
   │             // Evaluate each question response and calculate the total grade.\n
   │             foreach ($questions as $response) {\n
   │                 $result = self::gradeQuestion($studentDBConnection, $response, $schemaName, $sqlab);\n
   │                 $questionGrade = (float) $result['grade'];\n
   │ \n
   │                 // Store the individual grades and feedback for each response.\n
   │                 $DB->set_field('sqlab_responses', 'gradeobtained', $questionGrade, ['id' => $response->id]);\n
   │                 $DB->set_field('sqlab_responses', 'feedback', $result['feedback'], ['id' => $response->id]);\n
   │ \n
   │                 $totalGrade += $questionGrade;\n
   │             }\n
   │ \n
   │             // Update the total grade for the attempt in the database.\n
   │             $DB->set_field('sqlab_attempts', 'sumgrades', $totalGrade, ['id' => $attemptid]);\n
   │ \n
   │             // Set flag to true as all operations completed successfully.\n
   │             $deleteSchema = true;\n
   │ \n
   │         } catch (\Exception $e) {\n
   │             throw new \Exception($e->getMessage());\n
   │         } finally {\n
   │             // Conditionally drop the schema if all operations were successful.\n
   │             if ($deleteSchema) {\n
   │                 schema_manager::drop_schema($studentDBConnection, $schemaName);\n
   │             }\n
   │ \n
   │             // Always close the database connection to free resources.\n
   │             $dbConnector->closeConnection();\n
   │         }\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     /**\n
   │      * Grades an individual question based on the student's SQL response.\n
   │      *\n
   │      * @param resource $dbConnection The database connection resource.\n
   │      * @param stdClass $response The response object containing details like the student's submitted answer.\n
   │      * @param string $schemaName The name of the database schema where the queries are to be executed.\n
   │      * @param stdClass $sqlab Instance data containing quiz and question identifiers.\n
   │      * @return array Returns an array with 'grade' and 'feedback' keys.\n
   │      * @throws \moodle_exception Throws moodle_exception for specific errors controlled by the application.\n
   │      * @throws \Exception Throws generic Exception for uncontrolled or external errors.\n
   │      */\n
   │     protected static function gradeQuestion($dbConnection, $response, $schemaName, $sqlab)\n
   │     {\n
   │         // Return zero grade if student's response is empty.\n
   │         if (empty($response->response)) {\n
   │             return ['grade' => 0.0, 'feedback' => get_string('no_response_feedback', 'sqlab')];\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         // Get all questions from the quiz.\n
   │         $quiz_questions = sqlab_get_quiz_questions($sqlab->quizid);\n
   │ \n
   │         if (empty($quiz_questions)) {\n
   │             throw new \moodle_exception('noquestionsfound', 'sqlab');\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         // Find the specific question for the current response.\n
   │         $question = null;\n
   │         foreach ($quiz_questions as $q) {\n
   │             if ($q['questionid'] == $response->questionid) {\n
   │                 $question = $q;\n
   │                 break;\n
   │             }\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         if (!$question) {\n
   │             throw new \moodle_exception('questionnotfound', 'sqlab');\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         // Calculate the total penalty for executions.\n
   │         $totalDecrease = (float) $response->execution_count * $question['decreaseattempt'];\n
   │ \n
   │         // Calculate the new maximum possible score after the penalty.\n
   │         $newMaxGrade = (float) $response->currentmaxgrade - $totalDecrease;\n
   │ \n
   │         // Ensure that the new maximum grade is not lower than the minimum grade allowed.\n
   │         $maxGrade = (float) max($newMaxGrade, $question['mingrade']);\n
   │ \n
   │         // Generate and prepare relational schema and data if available.\n
   │         if (!empty($question['relationalschema'])) {\n
   │             internal_sql_executor::execute($response->userid, $question['relationalschema'], $schemaName, false, $dbConnection);\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         if (!empty($question['data'])) {\n
   │             internal_sql_executor::execute($response->userid, $question['data'], $schemaName, false, $dbConnection);\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         // Create the solution given by the student in the clean database.\n
   │         internal_sql_executor::execute($response->userid, $response->response, $schemaName, false, $dbConnection);\n
   │ \n
   │         // Create the function 'compare_views_with_order_and_diff'.\n
   │         self::generateEvaluatorFunction($dbConnection);\n
   │ \n
   │         // Create the views.\n
   │         internal_sql_executor::execute($response->userid, $question['sqlcheck'], $schemaName, false, $dbConnection);\n
   │ \n
   │         // Compare the views using the SQL function.\n
   │         $result = pg_query($dbConnection, $question['sqlcheckrun']);\n
   │ \n
   │         if (!$result) {\n
   │             $error = pg_last_error($dbConnection);\n
   │             throw new \Exception($error);\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         // Using regular expression to extract view names.\n
   │         if (preg_match("/compare_views_with_order_and_diff\('(.+?)', '(.+?)'\)/", $question['sqlcheckrun'], $matches) && count($matches) === 3) {\n
   │             $view1 = $matches[1];\n
   │             $view2 = $matches[2];\n
   │         } else {\n
   │             // Throw an exception if the names of the views could not be extracted from the query.\n
   │             throw new \moodle_exception('view_names_not_found', 'sqlab');\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         $allRowsCorrect = true; // Initialize flag to true, assuming all rows are initially correct.\n
   │         $feedbackDetails = []; // Array to store HTML details for feedback.\n
   │         $rows = []; // Array to store each row's HTML representation.\n
   │ \n
   │         while ($row = pg_fetch_assoc($result)) {\n
   │ \n
   │             if ($row['is_row_correct'] !== 't') {\n
   │                 $allRowsCorrect = false; // Set flag to false if any row is not correct.\n
   │             }\n
   │ \n
   │             // Construct row HTML for display.\n
   │             $rows[] = "<tr class='sql-results-row'>\n" .\n
   │                 "<td class='sql-results-data'>{$row['norder']}</td>\n" .\n
   │                 "<td class='sql-results-data'>" . ($row['is_row_correct'] === 't' ? get_string('yes', 'sqlab') : get_string('no', 'sqlab')) . "</td>\n" .\n
   │                 "<td class='sql-results-data'>{$row['is_in_solution']}</td>\n" .\n
   │                 "<td class='sql-results-data'>" . ($row['view1_row'] ? htmlspecialchars($row['view1_row']) : get_string('not_present', 'sqlab')) . "</td>\n" .\n
   │                 "<td class='sql-results-data'>" . ($row['view2_row'] ? htmlspecialchars($row['view2_row']) : get_string('not_present', 'sqlab')) . "</td>\n" .\n
   │                 "</tr>\n";\n
   │ \n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         if (!$allRowsCorrect) {\n
   │ \n
   │             // Add table header.\n
   │             $feedbackDetails[] = "<table class='sql-query-results'>\n" .\n
   │                 "<tr class='sql-results-header'>\n" .\n
   │                 "<th class='sql-results-header'>" . get_string('row', 'sqlab') . "</th>\n" .\n
   │                 "<th class='sql-results-header'>" . get_string('is_correct', 'sqlab') . "</th>\n" .\n
   │                 "<th class='sql-results-header'>" . get_string('status', 'sqlab') . "</th>\n" .\n
   │                 "<th class='sql-results-header'>" . get_string('your_answer', 'sqlab') . "</th>\n" .\n
   │                 "<th class='sql-results-header'>" . get_string('expected_answer', 'sqlab') . "</th>\n" .\n
   │                 "</tr>\n";\n
   │ \n
   │             // Add rows to the table.\n
   │             foreach ($rows as $rowHtml) {\n
   │                 $feedbackDetails[] = $rowHtml;\n
   │             }\n
   │ \n
   │             // Close the HTML table structure.\n
   │             $feedbackDetails[] = "</table>\n";\n
   │ \n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         // Clean up views to avoid future conflicts.\n
   │         pg_query($dbConnection, "DROP VIEW IF EXISTS $view1, $view2;");\n
   │ \n
   │         // Return the results of the comparison and the score.\n
   │         if ($allRowsCorrect) {\n
   │             return ['grade' => $maxGrade, 'feedback' => get_string('all_rows_correct_feedback', 'sqlab')];\n
   │         } else {\n
   │             $detailedFeedback = implode("\n", $feedbackDetails);\n
   │             return ['grade' => 0.0, 'feedback' => $detailedFeedback];\n
   │         }\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     /**\n
   │      * Ensures the evaluator function is present in the PostgreSQL database.\n
   │      * If the function does not exist, it is created from an SQL file.\n
   │      *\n
   │      * @param resource $dbConnection The database connection resource.\n
   │      * @throws \moodle_exception Throws moodle_exception for specific errors controlled by the application.\n
   │      */\n
   │     protected static function generateEvaluatorFunction($dbConnection)\n
   │     {\n
   │         // Define the path to the SQL file containing the function definition.\n
   │         $functionSqlPath = __DIR__ . '/../db/functions.sql';\n
   │ \n
   │         // Check if the SQL file exists and throw an exception if not.\n
   │         if (!file_exists($functionSqlPath)) {\n
   │             throw new \moodle_exception('sql_file_not_exist', 'sqlab', '', null, $functionSqlPath);\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         // Load the SQL query from the file.\n
   │         $functionSql = file_get_contents($functionSqlPath);\n
   │         if (!$functionSql) {\n
   │             throw new \moodle_exception('unable_to_load_sql', 'sqlab');\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         // Create or replace the function in the database.\n
   │         $createFunction = pg_query($dbConnection, $functionSql);\n
   │         if (!$createFunction) {\n
   │             throw new \moodle_exception('function_creation_failed', 'sqlab', '', null, pg_last_error($dbConnection));\n
   │         }\n
   │     }\n
   │ }\n
   │ <?php\n
   │ \n
   │ // Load the necessary configuration, library files and namespaces.\n
   │ require_once dirname(__FILE__) . '/../../config.php';\n
   │ require_once dirname(__FILE__) . '/lib.php';\n
   │ use mod_sqlab\schema_manager;\n
   │ use mod_sqlab\internal_sql_executor;\n
   │ use mod_sqlab\attempt_manager;\n
   │ \n
   │ try {\n
   │ \n
   │     // Fetch and validate the necessary parameter from the request.\n
   │     $cmid = optional_param('cmid', null, PARAM_INT);\n
   │ \n
   │     // Validate course module and additional data.\n
   │     if ($cmid === null) {\n
   │         throw new moodle_exception('nocmid', 'sqlab');\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     $cm = get_coursemodule_from_id('sqlab', $cmid);\n
   │     if (!$cm) {\n
   │         throw new moodle_exception('invalidcoursemodule', 'sqlab');\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     $course = get_course($cm->course);\n
   │     if (!$course) {\n
   │         throw new moodle_exception('invalidcourseid', 'sqlab');\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     // Get and check the existence of the SQLab instance.\n
   │     $sqlab = $DB->get_record('sqlab', array('id' => $cm->instance), '*', IGNORE_MISSING);\n
   │     if (!$sqlab) {\n
   │         throw new moodle_exception('invalidsqlabid', 'sqlab');\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │ } catch (moodle_exception $e) {\n
   │ \n
   │     // Define the redirect URL.\n
   │     $redirectUrl = (!empty($course->id)) ? new moodle_url('/course/view.php', ['id' => $course->id]) : new moodle_url('/my/');\n
   │ \n
   │     \core\notification::error(get_string($e->errorcode, $e->module));\n
   │     redirect($redirectUrl);\n
   │     exit;\n
   │ \n
   │ }\n
   │ \n
   │ // Enforce user login, course module context and check capabilities.\n
   │ $context = context_module::instance($cm->id);\n
   │ require_login($course, true, $cm);\n
   │ require_capability('mod/sqlab:view', $context);\n
   │ require_capability('mod/sqlab:attempt', $context);\n
   │ \n
   │ // Check if the 'action' POST parameter is set and if the action is to 'create_new_attempt'.\n
   │ if (isset($_POST['action']) && $_POST['action'] === 'create_new_attempt') {\n
   │ \n
   │     try {\n
   │ \n
   │         // Create a new attempt using the attempt manager class with the necessary IDs.\n
   │         $newattemptid = attempt_manager::create_new_attempt($sqlab->id, $USER->id);\n
   │ \n
   │         // Handle the setup for the first attempt.\n
   │         schema_manager::handle_first_attempt($newattemptid, $USER->id);\n
   │ \n
   │         // Retrieve quiz questions.\n
   │         $quiz_questions = sqlab_get_quiz_questions($sqlab->quizid);\n
   │ \n
   │         // Check if there are no quiz questions returned.\n
   │         if (empty($quiz_questions)) {\n
   │             echo json_encode(['status' => 'error', 'message' => get_string('noquestionsfound', 'sqlab')]);\n
   │             exit;\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         // Format the schema name based on the SQLab name.\n
   │         $schemaName = schema_manager::format_activity_name($sqlab->name);\n
   │ \n
   │         // Create the relational schema for each question.\n
   │         foreach ($quiz_questions as $question) {\n
   │             internal_sql_executor::execute($USER->id, $question['relationalschema'], $schemaName, false, null, false);\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         // Prepare the context for each question, inserting data into the relational schema.\n
   │         foreach ($quiz_questions as $question) {\n
   │             internal_sql_executor::execute($USER->id, $question['data'], $schemaName);\n
   │         }\n
   │ \n
   │         // Respond with a success status and include the new attempt ID.\n
   │         echo json_encode(['status' => 'success', 'newattemptid' => $newattemptid]);\n
   │ \n
   │     } catch (Exception $e) {\n
   │ \n
   │         // Catch any exceptions that occur during the attempt creation and respond with an error.\n
   │         echo json_encode(['status' => 'error', 'message' => $e->getMessage()]);\n
   │         exit;\n
   │ \n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │ } else {\n
   │ \n
   │     // Respond with an error if the 'action' parameter is not set or not equal to 'create_new_attempt'.\n
   │     echo json_encode(['status' => 'error', 'message' => 'Invalid request']);\n
   │     exit;\n
   │ \n
   │ }\n

   │ <?php\n
   │ \n
   │ // Load the necessary configuration and library files.\n
   │ require_once dirname(__FILE__) . '/../../config.php';\n
   │ require_once dirname(__FILE__) . '/lib.php';\n
   │ \n
   │ try {\n
   │ \n
   │     // Fetch necessary parameters from the request.\n
   │     $attemptid = optional_param('attempt', null, PARAM_INT);\n
   │     $cmid = optional_param('cmid', null, PARAM_INT);\n
   │ \n
   │     // Validate course module and additional data.\n
   │     if ($cmid === null) {\n
   │         throw new moodle_exception('nocmid', 'sqlab');\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n

   │         throw new moodle_exception('invalidsqlabid', 'sqlab');\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n

   │         throw new moodle_exception('invalidattemptid', 'sqlab');\n
   │     }\n

   │         $redirectUrl = new moodle_url('/my/');\n
   │     } else if ($e->errorcode === 'invalidsqlabid') {\n
   │         $redirectUrl = new moodle_url('/my/');\n

   │         if (!empty($cmid)) {\n
   │             $redirectUrl = new moodle_url('/mod/sqlab/view.php', ['id' => $cmid]);  // Redirect to the module's view page if cmid is available and valid.\n

   │         array(\n
   │             $index + 1,\n
   │             $question_state\n

   │ // Set the content type of the response to JSON.\n

   │ try {\n
   │ \n

   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     // Retrieve JSON input from the request body and decode it.\n
   │     $json_input = file_get_contents('php://input');\n
   │     $input = json_decode($json_input, true);\n
   │ \n
   │     // Check if all required parameters are provided.\n
   │     if (!isset($input['userId']) || !isset($input['sql']) || !isset($input['schemaName'])) {\n
   │         throw new moodle_exception('missingparameters', 'sqlab');\n
   │     }\n
   │ \n
   │     // Extract parameters from the input.\n
   │     $userId = $input['userId'];\n
   │     $sql = $input['sql'];\n
   │     $schemaName = $input['schemaName'];\n
   │     $fetchResults = $input['fetchResults'] ?? false;\n
   │ \n
   │     // Execute the SQL query using the provided parameters and fetch option.\n
   │     $results = internal_sql_executor::execute($userId, $sql, $schemaName, $fetchResults);\n
   │ \n
   │     // Output the success status and query results as JSON.\n
   │     echo json_encode([\n
   │         'status' => 'success',\n
   │         'results' => $results\n
   │     ]);\n
   │ \n

   │         'status' => 'error',\n
